fame, strength, family, and friendship from the lead singer of TLC<p>As the lead singer of Grammy-winning supergroup TLC, Tionne "T-Boz" Watkins has seen phenomenal fame, success, and critical acclaim. But backstage, she has lived a dual life. In addition to the balancing act of juggling an all-consuming music career and her family, Tionne has struggled since she was a young girl with sickle-cell disease--a debilitating and incurable condition that can render her unable to perform, walk, or even breathe.</p><p>A Sick Life chronicles Tionne's journey from a sickly young girl from Des Moines who was told she wouldn't live to see 30 through her teen years in Atlanta, how she broke into the music scene, and became the superstar musician and sickle-cell disease advocate she is today. Through Tionne's tough, funny, tell-it-like-it-is voice, she shares how she found the inner strength, grit, and determination to live her dream, despite her often unpredictable and debilitating health issues. She dives deep into never-before-told TLC stories, including accounts of her friendship with Lisa "Left-Eye" Lopes and her tragic death. Tionne's unvarnished discussion of her remarkable life, disease, unending strength, and ability to power through the odds offers a story like no other.</p> <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <a class="full-title">Defining Moments in Black History: Reading Between the Lies</span> <span class="paragraph-end"></span> </a> <div class="subtitle-container"> <a class="subtitle author has-pub-date non-comic-series" href="/store/books/author?id=Dick+Gregory" title="Dick Gregory">Dick Gregory</a> <a class="subtitle pub-date non-comic-series" href="/store/books/details/Dick_Gregory_Defining_Moments_in_Black_History?id=10PKDQAAQBAJ" title="September 5, 2017">September 5, 2017</a> <span class="price-container"> <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <span class="books is-price-tag buy-button-container is_not_aquired_or_preordered" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="book-10PKDQAAQBAJ"> <div class="pon" style="display:none">2</div> <button class="price buy id-track-click id-track-impression" data-server-cookie="CAIaKwoUEhIKDDEwUEtEUUFBUUJBShAFGAEyEwio+MKb3/vWAhXQ3CUKHRriDZ8=" data-uitype="200"> <span class="display-price">$12.99</span> </button> </span> </span> </div> <div class="description">  With his trademark acerbic wit, incisive humor, and infectious paranoia, one of our foremost comedians and most politically engaged civil rights activists looks back at 100 key events from the complicated history of black America.<p>A friend of luminaries including Dr. Martin Luther King, Jr. and Medgar Evers, and the forebear of today&#8217;s popular black comics, including Larry Wilmore, W. Kamau Bell, Damon Young, and Trevor Noah, Dick Gregory was a provocative and incisive cultural force for more than fifty years. As an entertainer, he always kept it indisputably real about race issues in America, fearlessly lacing laughter with hard truths. As a leading activist against injustice, he marched at Selma during the Civil Rights movement, organized student rallies to protest the Vietnam War; sat in at rallies for Native American and feminist rights; fought apartheid in South Africa; and participated in hunger strikes in support of Black Lives Matter. </p><p>In this collection of thoughtful, provocative essays, Gregory charts the complex and often obscured history of the African American experience. In his unapologetically candid voice, he moves from African ancestry and surviving the Middle Passage to the creation of the Jheri Curl, the enjoyment of bacon and everything pig, the headline-making shootings of black men, and the Black Lives Matter movement. A captivating journey through time, Defining Moments in Black History explores historical movements such as The Great Migration and the Harlem Renaissance, as well as cultural touchstones such as Sidney Poitier winning the Best Actor Oscar for Lilies in the Field and Billie Holiday releasing Strange Fruit. </p><p>An engaging look at black life that offers insightful commentary on the intricate history of the African American people, Defining Moments in Black History is an essential, no-holds-bar history lesson that will provoke, enlighten, and entertain. </p> <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <a aria-hidden="true" class="card-click-target" href="/store/books/details/Dick_Gregory_Defining_Moments_in_Black_History?id=10PKDQAAQBAJ" tabindex="-1"> </a> </div> Dangerous Situation"> <span class="full-title">100 Deadly Skills: The SEAL Operative's Guide to Eluding Pursuers, Evading Capture, and Surviving Any Dangerous Situation</span> <span class="paragraph-end"></span> </a> <div class="subtitle-container"> <a class="subtitle author has-pub-date non-comic-series" href="/store/info/name/Clint_Emerson?id=11byth90xk" title="Clint Emerson">Clint Emerson</a> <a class="subtitle pub-date non-comic-series" href="/store/books/details/Clint_Emerson_100_Deadly_Skills?id=qLv_BgAAQBAJ" title="October 13, 2015">October 13, 2015</a> <span class="price-container"> <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <span class="books is-price-tag buy-button-container is_not_aquired_or_preordered" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="book-qLv_BgAAQBAJ"> <div class="pon" style="display:none">2</div> <button class="price buy id-track-click id-track-impression" data-server-cookie="CAIaKwoUEhIKDHFMdl9CZ0FBUUJBShAFGAEyEwio+MKb3/vWAhXQ3CUKHRriDZ8=" data-uitype="200"> <span class="display-price">$14.99</span> </button> </span> </span> </div> <div class="description">  A hands-on, practical survival guide from retired Navy SEAL Clint Emerson&#8212;adapted for civilians from actual special forces operations&#8212;to eluding pursuers, evading capture, and surviving any dangerous situation.<br/><br/>In today&#8217;s increasingly dangerous world, threats to your personal safety are everywhere. From acts of terror to mass shootings, and from the unseen (and sometimes virtual) matrix of everyday crime, danger is no longer confined to dark alleys or unstable regions. Potentially life-threatening circumstances can arise anywhere, anytime, and Clint Emerson&#8212;former Navy SEAL&#8212;wants you to be prepared.<br/> <br/>100 Deadly Skills contains proven self-defense skills, evasion tactics, and immobilizing maneuvers&#8212;modified from the world of black ops&#8212;to help you take action in numerous &#8220;worst case&#8221; scenarios from escaping a locked trunk, to making an improvised Taser, to tricking facial recognition software. With easy-to-understand instructions and illustrations, Emerson outlines in detail many life-saving strategies and teaches you how to think and act like a member of the special forces.<br/> <br/>This complete course in survival teaches you how to prevent tracking, evade a kidnapping, elude an active shooter, rappel down the side of a building, immobilize a bad guy, protect yourself against cyber-criminals, and much more&#8212;all using low-tech to &#8220;no-tech&#8221; methods. Clear, detailed, and presented in an easy-to-understand and execute format, 100 Deadly Skills is an invaluable resource. </div> <div class="description">  Evolve is the third studio album by American rock band Imagine Dragons, released on June 23, 2017 through KIDinaKORNER and Interscope Records. The album is the band's new material follow-up to their second studio album, Smoke + Mirrors.<br/>After the release of Smoke + Mirrors and its respective world tour, a self-imposed hiatus for 2016 and cryptic messages from the band through their social media gained anticipation for their third album. The album was finally announced on May 9, with the initiation of the album's pre-order. In comparison to Night Visions and Smoke + Mirrors, frontman Dan Reynolds explained that the album will be an 'evolution for Imagine Dragons'.<br/>The album was promoted by two singles: "Believer" and "Thunder" as well as an upcoming tour produced by Live Nation and supported with Grouplove and K.Flay will start in September 2017. <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <a aria-hidden="true" href="/store/music/album/Tom_Petty_And_The_Heartbreakers_Greatest_Hits?id=Ba5hswi5cnngye7ligfa3lnub5u" tabindex="-1" title="Greatest Hits">  Greatest Hits <span class="paragraph-end"></span> </a> <div class="subtitle-container"> <a class="subtitle" href="/store/music/artist/Tom_Petty_And_The_Heartbreakers?id=Ag5n7etpdn72i5cr6ltlaljxm3u" title="Tom Petty And The Heartbreakers">Tom Petty And The Heartbreakers</a> <span class="price-container"> <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <span class="music is-price-tag buy-button-container is_not_aquired_or_preordered" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="album-Ba5hswi5cnngye7ligfa3lnub5u"> <div class="pon" style="display:none">1</div> <button class="price buy id-track-click id-track-impression" data-server-cookie="CAIaPAojEiEKG0JhNWhzd2k1Y25uZ3llN2xpZ2ZhM2xudWI1dRACGAIyEwio+MKb3/vWAhXQ3CUKHRriDZ9CAA==" data-uitype="200"> <span class="display-price">$8.99</span> </button> </span> </span> </div> <div class="description">  Greatest Hits is a compilation album by Tom Petty and the Heartbreakers, released in 1993. It is Petty's best-selling album to date and was certified 12&#215; platinum by the RIAA on April 28, 2015. The single "Mary Jane's Last Dance" became one of Petty's most popular songs, reaching #14 on the Billboard Hot 100 and #1 on the Billboard Mainstream Rock Tracks chart. The other new song on the album is a cover of the Thunderclap Newman hit "Something in the Air". The album contains no songs from 1987's Let Me Up. However, three songs from 1989's Full Moon Fever were included; despite the album's technical status as a Tom Petty solo album, it contained contributions from several members from the Heartbreakers, thus legitimizing its inclusion on this compilation. As of September 2011, Greatest Hits had sold 7,464,000 copies in the United States, making it Tom Petty's best-selling album. <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <a aria-hidden="true" class="card-click-target" href="/store/music/album/Tom_Petty_And_The_Heartbreakers_Greatest_Hits?id=Ba5hswi5cnngye7ligfa3lnub5u" tabindex="-1"> </a> </div> </div> <div class="reason-set"> <span She chooses the Metropolitan Museum of Art in New York City. Knowing that her younger brother Jamie has money and thus can help her with a serious cash-flow problem, she invites him along.<br/> <br/>Once settled into the museum, Claudia and Jamie find themselves caught up in the mystery of an angel statue that the museum purchased at auction for a bargain price of $225.
